Session Number: 70

Chapter: Chapter 5 : The Knight and the Dragon

Key Locations: the DMZ between Silverrige and Montimer

Media:

Players Attending:

# Synopsis

Casimir prepares to speak with Kristjan Covinggard, framing the conversation as neighbors' discourse rather than a covert negotiation for a potential invasion into Rivers. Sovereign accompanies him to facilitate talks between "Rivers Durand" and the Blood Prince.

Kristjan reveals a somewhat positive relationship with Endi and Sherman, or at least what he publicly admits. Sovereign interjects with a platitude about maintaining friendships despite differing opinions on power dynamics. The conversation shifts to Casimir's time as a Crusader, with a focus on the exotic lands of the Mikado rather than the details of the Crusades.

Kristjan offers to eliminate Donald Durand, who attempted to harm Casimir's wife, indicating political imprisonments in Covenguard. Meanwhile, Caden follows a random bloody trail, and a wounded bobcat is tended to and given Caden's scent for future identification.

During a river journey, an overarching discussion ensues about Montmier. Although heated, no concrete decision is reached, emphasizing the importance of making friends with minor houses over making enemies of major ones. Upon disembarking, a military contingent is encountered, prompting Casimir and Caden to befriend them for safer travel.

Oliwier Sobczak, a key figure in Montimer culture, welcomes the group and emphasizes the significance of knighthood within the Ashen Order. Colonel Kamil Krupa provides insight into the Red Spot and its members. Lady Deva, a formidable horse archer, impresses the group, and a secret phrase supporting Talmert expansion is revealed.

Abagail Trudo discusses training methods with Casimir, expressing feeling abandoned by the Tested and subsequently joining the Knights of Montimer. Sovereign learns more about her rings, signifying Language Saltblood, Lore Valves of the Heartstone, and Warfare.

Peter McBravo engages with Sir Emil Shäffer, a Red Spot envoy, and Shivon charms Colonel Kamil Krupa, learning about the Hussars' frustrations in the region. Igor Nowicki shares information about Hans being captured by "Almerin heretics" in the unruly lands of northern Almerin.

At midnight, a toast is given to Duchess Lucy, diverting from the expected Duke Charles, followed by toasts to Conner and Baby Angus.
